罢了罢了，是以如今，我不体谅你，你不原谅我，又何苦互相在纠缠，只想与你说。

Bãi liễu bãi liễu, thị dĩ như kim, ngã bất thể lượng nhĩ, nhĩ bất nguyên lượng ngã, hựu hà khổ hỗ tương tại củ triền, chỉ tưởng dữ nhĩ thuyết.

Thôi thôi, này đây hiện giờ, ta không thông cảm ngươi, ngươi không tha thứ ta, làm sao khổ cho nhau ở dây dưa, chỉ nghĩ nói với ngươi.

that's all, now, i don't understand you, you don't forgive me, and why bother with each other, i just want to talk to you.

他日，若嫁作人妇，可得改了这作脾气，女人娇点男人才疼得下去。

Tha nhật, nhược giá tác nhân phụ, khả đắc cải liễu giá tác tì khí, nữ nhân kiều điểm nam nhân tài đông đắc hạ khứ.

Ngày nào đó, nếu gả làm người phụ, nhưng đến sửa lại này làm tính tình, nữ nhân kiều điểm nam nhân mới đau đến đi xuống.

if he marries a woman, he will have to change his temper, and the woman will be able to hurt a man.

罢了，除了我，也没人受得了你这破脾气。

Bãi liễu, trừ liễu ngã, dã một nhân thụ đắc liễu nhĩ giá phá tì khí.

Thôi, trừ bỏ ta, cũng không ai chịu được ngươi này phá tính tình.

except for me, no one can stand your broken temper.

想我时……算了，别想我，你想我我也不会出现在你的面前，凭添烦恼，如若要是下桥时能见到那孟婆，我去与她讨一碗汤喝，夜里入梦让你喝了，把咱这前尘往事都给了了。

Tưởng ngã thời…… Toán liễu, biệt tưởng ngã, nhĩ tưởng ngã ngã dã bất hội xuất hiện tại nhĩ đích diện tiền, bằng thiêm phiền não, như nhược yếu thị hạ kiều thời năng kiến đáo na mạnh bà, ngã khứ dữ tha thảo nhất oản thang hát, dạ lí nhập mộng nhượng nhĩ hát liễu, bả cha giá tiền trần vãng sự đô cấp liễu liễu.

Tưởng ta khi…… Tính, đừng nghĩ ta, ngươi tưởng ta ta cũng sẽ không xuất hiện ở ngươi trước mặt, bằng thêm phiền não, nếu như nếu là hạ kiều khi có thể nhìn thấy kia Mạnh Bà, ta đi cùng nàng thảo một chén canh uống, ban đêm đi vào giấc mộng làm ngươi uống, đem ta này chuyện cũ năm xưa đều cho.

when thinking of me... forget it, don't think about me, you think i won't appear in front of you, with added troubles, such as if i can see na meng po when i get off the bridge, i will go to ask her for a bowl of soup to drink, and i will let you drink it at night, and give us all the dust of the past.

我走了才能放心些。

Ngã tẩu liễu tài năng phóng tâm ta.

Ta đi rồi mới có thể yên tâm chút.

i'm leaving to be relieved.

有些话，在时没能与你说，死了更不会说，所以，你想听的那句没有，有的只是一句，好好保重身体，别太早来见我。

Hữu ta thoại, tại thời một năng dữ nhĩ thuyết, tử liễu canh bất hội thuyết, sở dĩ, nhĩ tưởng thính đích na cú một hữu, hữu đích chỉ thị nhất cú, hảo hảo bảo trọng thân thể, biệt thái tảo lai kiến ngã.

Có chút lời nói, ở khi không có thể nói với ngươi, đã chết càng sẽ không nói, cho nên, ngươi muốn nghe câu kia không có, có chỉ là một câu, hảo hảo bảo trọng thân thể, đừng quá sớm tới gặp ta.

some words, when you can't say it to you, let alone say it when you're dead, so the one you want to hear is not, some are just a sentence, take good care of your body, don't come to see me too early.

否则，也不会理你。

Phủ tắc, dã bất hội lý nhĩ.

Nếu không, cũng sẽ không lý ngươi.

otherwise, it won't bother you.

如果有下辈子，我还是会当兵，如若遇上我，你还是绕道走吧。”

Như quả hữu hạ bối tử, ngã hoàn thị hội đương binh, như nhược ngộ thượng ngã, nhĩ hoàn thị nhiễu đạo tẩu ba.”

Nếu có kiếp sau, ta còn là sẽ tham gia quân ngũ, nếu như gặp gỡ ta, ngươi vẫn là đường vòng đi thôi.”

if there is a next life, i will still be a soldier, if you meet me, you still have to take a detour. ”

如果说这封书信是林清远假造的，南月如是绝对不会相信的，这字里行间全是那男人平日里说话的口气，所以他俩这误会真要下地下去解说了。

Như quả thuyết giá phong thư tín thị lâm thanh viễn giả tạo đích, nam nguyệt như thị tuyệt đối bất hội tương tín đích, giá tự lí hành gian toàn thị na nam nhân bình nhật lí thuyết thoại đích khẩu khí, sở dĩ tha lưỡng giá ngộ hội chân yếu hạ địa hạ khứ giải thuyết liễu.

Nếu nói này phong thư từ là Lâm Thanh Viễn giả tạo, Nam Nguyệt Như là tuyệt đối sẽ không tin tưởng, này giữa những hàng chữ tất cả đều là kia nam nhân ngày thường nói chuyện khẩu khí, cho nên hai người bọn họ này hiểu lầm thật muốn xuống đất đi xuống giải thích.

if this letter was forged by lin qingyuan, nan yueru would never believe it, and the words between the lines were all the tone of the man's usual speech, so they really had to go down to the ground to explain this misunderstanding.

她坐在位置上，一会儿哭一会笑，一会儿把纸张揉碎，因为话里字里行间全是欠扁的想让她揍他，可觉得这就是活生生的他，她又摊开抚平，手指在那一条条折痕上眷恋地轻轻拂过。

Nàng ngồi ở vị trí thượng, trong chốc lát khóc một hồi cười, trong chốc lát đem trang giấy xoa nát, bởi vì lời nói giữa những hàng chữ tất cả đều là thiếu đánh muốn cho nàng tấu hắn, cảm nhận được đến đây là sống sờ sờ hắn, nàng lại mở ra vuốt phẳng, ngón tay ở kia từng điều nếp gấp thượng quyến luyến mà nhẹ nhàng phất quá.

she sat in her place, crying and laughing for a while, and crushing the paper for a while, because the words were full of flattening and wanting her to beat him, but she felt that this was the living him, and she spread out and smoothed it out, and her fingers brushed lovingly on the creases.

她跟疯了似的，哭哭笑笑，抹干眼泪，攥紧这世间他留下最后的东西。

Tha cân phong liễu tự đích, khóc khóc tiếu tiếu, mạt càn nhãn lệ, toản khẩn giá thế gian tha lưu hạ tối hậu đích đông tây.

Nàng cùng điên rồi dường như, khóc khóc cười cười, mạt làm nước mắt, nắm chặt thế gian này hắn lưu lại cuối cùng đồ vật.

she was like crazy, crying and laughing, wiping away her tears, clutching the last thing he had left behind in this world.

林陆骁回去的时候，南初正伏案跪在地板上写东西。

when lin luxiao returned, nan chu was kneeling on the floor to write something.

听到声音，头也没抬，埋头继续写，漫不经心地说：“回来啦？”

hearing the voice, he didn't raise his head, buried his head and continued to write, casually saying: "come back?" ”

男人低嗯一声，放下手里的东西，走过去抱她，把她搂进怀里，低头吻她，“在写什么？”

the man muttered a low, put down what was in his hand, walked over and hugged her, took her into his arms, and looked down and kissed her, "what are you writing?" ”

南初把稿子往身后一藏，仰头去回吻他：“下回再给你看。”

nanchu hid the manuscript behind him, looked up and kissed him back: "i'll show it to you next time." ”

lin luxiao smiled, beat her up, the field of vision was suddenly wide, nanchu discovered the new continent, and pointed at the table: "oh oh oh!!! what is that? ”

their lives were not as good as these things.

"how?" nan chu glanced at lin luxiao and asked the doctor.

the doctor all rolled around and pushed his glasses, "very good, your husband is no problem." you both have no problem, don't be too anxious, want the child to see the opportunity. and you are still so young, there is no hurry in a few years. ”

Nam Sơ do dự mà nói: “Nhưng ta lão công tuổi lớn.”

nanchu said hesitantly, "but my husband is older." ”

the doctor glanced at the handsome man next to him, "not big." ”

Nam Sơ: “Nghe nói nam nhân thượng 30, chất lượng liền không được như xưa.”

nanchu: "i heard that men are thirty years old, and the quality is not as good as before." ”

the doctor rolled his eyes: "don't be too demanding, the children born of thirty-five also have smart decisions, this depends on the individual." ”

林陆骁冷笑地坐在位置上。

Lâm lục kiêu lãnh tiếu địa tọa tại vị trí thượng.

Lâm Lục Kiêu cười lạnh mà ngồi ở vị trí thượng.

lin luxiao sneered and sat in his seat.

出了院门，他一把给人拎进去，“年纪大，质量不如从前？看来我最近的表现你很不满意啊。”

out of the courtyard door, he carried someone in, "old, the quality is not as good as before?" it seems that you are very dissatisfied with my recent performance. ”

nanchu has hardly taken over the drama recently, and she doesn't care much about things in the circle, and her heart is on her flower shop.

this circle, coming and going, so many people, can remember a few people.

it's funny to think about it.

so when waiting in the background, bored with the mobile phone to search for the female star's photo to download it, put their own photos together, and sent them to lin luxiao, "husband, which is me?" ”

calm enough that people thought it was just a joke, but she didn't think that in fact, she had already said these words a thousand times on paper, waiting for one day to be publicly said to everyone.

“其实恋情曾被人公开过一次，那时有人攻击他，说他是最烂的兵种，他们把对我的恶意都转嫁到他跟他的父亲身上，当时不敢发声，我这人表达不好，越说越乱，越说越被人抓把柄，当时选择沉默，让舆论过去。”

“Kỳ thật luyến tình tằng bị nhân công khai quá nhất thứ, na thời hữu nhân công kích tha, thuyết tha thị tối lạn đích binh chủng, tha môn bả đối ngã đích ác ý đô chuyển giá đáo tha cân tha đích phụ thân thân thượng, đương thời bất cảm phát thanh, ngã giá nhân biểu đạt bất hảo, việt thuyết việt loạn, việt thuyết việt bị nhân trảo bả bính, đương thời tuyển trạch trầm mặc, nhượng dư luận quá khứ.”

“Kỳ thật tình yêu từng bị người công khai quá một lần, khi đó có người công kích hắn, nói hắn là nhất lạn binh chủng, bọn họ đem đối ta ác ý đều tái giá đến hắn cùng phụ thân hắn trên người, lúc ấy không dám phát ra tiếng, ta người này biểu đạt không tốt, càng nói càng loạn, càng nói càng bị người trảo nhược điểm, lúc ấy lựa chọn trầm mặc, làm dư luận qua đi.”

"in fact, the love affair was made public once, when some people attacked him, saying that he was the worst soldier, they transferred all their malice toward me to him and his father, at that time they did not dare to speak out, i was not a good expression, the more i said the more chaotic, the more i said the more people were caught, at that time chose to be silent, let public opinion pass."

她笑笑，继续说：“他父亲被气入院，当时是真怕，万一因为我有什么意外，我以后怎么面对他呀，胆小的我就跑了，跑到美国去上学了，半年内都不敢说话，出门都带着口罩帽子怕被人认出来，每每翻到那句最烂的兵种就跟扎在我心里的刀似的。”

Tha tiếu tiếu, kế tục thuyết: “Tha phụ thân bị khí nhập viện, đương thời thị chân phạ, vạn nhất nhân vi ngã hữu thập ma ý ngoại, ngã dĩ hậu chẩm ma diện đối tha nha, đảm tiểu đích ngã tựu bào liễu, bào đáo mỹ quốc khứ thượng học liễu, bán niên nội đô bất cảm thuyết thoại, xuất môn đô đái trứ khẩu tráo mạo tử phạ bị nhân nhận xuất lai, mỗi mỗi phiên đáo na cú tối lạn đích binh chủng tựu cân trát tại ngã tâm lí đích đao tự đích.”

Nàng cười cười, tiếp tục nói: “Phụ thân hắn bị khí nhập viện, lúc ấy là thật sợ, vạn nhất bởi vì ta có cái gì ngoài ý muốn, ta về sau như thế nào đối mặt hắn nha, nhát gan ta liền chạy, chạy đến nước Mỹ đi đi học, nửa năm nội cũng không dám nói chuyện, ra cửa đều mang theo khẩu trang mũ sợ bị người nhận ra tới, mỗi khi phiên đến câu kia nhất lạn binh chủng liền cùng trát ở lòng ta đao dường như.”

she smiled and continued: "his father was angry and hospitalized, at that time he was really afraid, in case i had any accidents, how would i face him in the future, i ran away, ran to the united states to go to school, did not dare to speak for half a year, went out with a mask and hat for fear of being recognized, and every time i turned over the worst soldiers, it was like a knife stuck in my heart." ”

“我曾参加过一个节目，不知道什么原因，那个节目最终没有播出，听说是投资人把节目给撤了，那是个消防节目，有机会的话，我觉得你们可以去了解了解，兵种没有什么烂不烂，都是中国军人，都在默默做着建设，都会有牺牲，都是为了我们，我说这些，不需要任何人的道歉，我只希望，未来的网络，对自己的言论，多点负责，少点暴力。”

“Ngã tằng tham gia quá nhất cá tiết mục, bất tri đạo thập ma nguyên nhân, na cá tiết mục tối chung một hữu bá xuất, thính thuyết thị đầu tư nhân bả tiết mục cấp triệt liễu, na thị cá tiêu phòng tiết mục, hữu cơ hội đích thoại, ngã giác đắc nhĩ môn khả dĩ khứ liễu giải liễu giải, binh chủng một hữu thập ma lạn bất lạn, đô thị trung quốc quân nhân, đô tại mặc mặc tố trứ kiến thiết, đô hội hữu hi sinh, đô thị vi liễu ngã môn, ngã thuyết giá ta, bất nhu yếu nhậm hà nhân đích đạo khiểm, ngã chỉ hi vọng, vị lai đích võng lạc, đối tự kỷ đích ngôn luận, đa điểm phụ trách, thiếu điểm bạo lực.”

“Ta từng tham gia quá một cái tiết mục, không biết cái gì nguyên nhân, cái kia tiết mục cuối cùng không có bá ra, nghe nói là đầu tư người đem tiết mục cấp triệt, đó là cái phòng cháy tiết mục, có cơ hội nói, ta cảm thấy các ngươi có thể đi hiểu biết hiểu biết, binh chủng không có gì lạn không lạn, đều là Trung Quốc quân nhân, đều ở yên lặng làm xây dựng, đều sẽ có hy sinh, đều là vì chúng ta, ta nói này đó, không cần bất luận kẻ nào xin lỗi, ta chỉ hy vọng, tương lai internet, đối chính mình ngôn luận, nhiều điểm phụ trách, thiếu điểm bạo lực.”

"i once participated in a program, i don't know what the reason is, that program was not broadcast in the end, i heard that the investors withdrew the program, it was a fire program, if there is a chance, i think you can understand and understand, there is nothing rotten in the military, all are chinese soldiers, they are silently doing construction, there will be sacrifices, all for us, i say this, do not need anyone's apology, i only hope that the future network, for their own speech, more responsible, less violence." 」

xi gu and yan dai are bridesmaids, living in nanchu's home a day early, tomorrow morning they have to get up to make up, wear clothes, a lot of things, plus recently xi gu and han beiyao have an awkward quarrel, has occupied a long room in nanchu's home, so that they can't help ... lin luxiao really wanted to throw people out every minute, but there was no way, nan chu san ling wu shen was kind to her friends, because she didn't have any friends.

南初朋友少，留在她身边的每一位她都很珍惜。

nanchu had few friends, and she cherished every one who stayed with her.

“你晚上住哪儿？”南初问。

"where do you stay at night?" nanchu asked.

林陆晓沿着栏杆的边沿磕了磕烟灰，淡笑说：“今晚估计没法睡了。”

lin luxiao bumped the soot along the edge of the railing, smiled lightly, and said, "i guess i can't sleep tonight."

“为什么？”

"why?"

“喝完这顿，还得去沈牧家。”

"after drinking this meal, i still have to go to shen mu's house."

“去干吗？”

"what are you going to do?"

他低头笑，“他俩说，明天我就正式脱单了，今晚得陪他俩打一晚上的小霸王。”

he looked down and smiled, "they said, tomorrow i will officially get off the list, and tonight i have to accompany them to play a night of little bully."

小霸王是那时候的街机，沈牧家里有一个，林陆晓艰大刘几个就天天蹲在他家打这游戏，都是小时候爱干的事，长大就少了，也没什么机会。

xiao bawang was an arcade machine at that time, shen mu's family had one, lin lu xiao was a few big liu squatting in his house every day to play this game, all of which were things he loved to do when he was a child, and when he grew up, there was less, and there was no chance.

结了婚就不一样了，有了媳妇儿，有了孩子。再想要这么玩儿几乎不可能了，于是今晚的行程都被大刘安安排得满满的，也算是帮他这兄弟践行。

getting married is different, having a daughter-in-law and having children. it is almost impossible to want to play like this again, so tonight's itinerary is full of arrangements by big liu an, which can also be regarded as helping his brother practice.

男人间的那股子情谊，女人是不懂的。

the friendship between men, women do not understand.

南初只担心林陆骁明天会不会太累，问：“明天吃得消吗？”

nan chu was only worried about whether lin luxiao would be too tired tomorrow and asked, "will you be able to eat tomorrow?"

结果这么简单的一问话，在某人耳朵里里就听成了有色的，坏笑着在电话那头问：“你是担心明天晚上吗？”

as a result, such a simple question was colored in someone's ear, and a bad smile asked on the other end of the phone: "are you worried about tomorrow night?"

“新婚之夜五分钟的话，我真的会笑你一辈子。”

"if it's five minutes on wedding night, i'll really laugh at you for the rest of my life."

林陆骁笑：“明天你别哭。”

lin luxiao smiled, "tomorrow you don't cry."

（4）

（4）

婚礼当天。

wedding day.

南初起了个大早，还不等她说话，西顾跟严黛已经吵上了，两人你一言我一语，丝毫没有她插话的空间。“这个头饰好看，配南初。”

nan chu got up early in the morning, before she could speak, xi gu and yan dai were already arguing, and the two of you said a word to me, and there was no room for her to interject. "this headdress looks good, with nanchu."

“不要！太老气了，这个好，这个清纯。”

"don't! too old-fashioned, this good, this pure.

“这双鞋子，配这双鞋子，比较亮。”

"these shoes, with these shoes, are brighter."

“不要，结婚就应该穿红色的！”

"no, you should wear red when you get married!"

这头闹着，那边也不轻松，婚礼办得比较低调，媒体记者统统被挡在门外，林清远早前派人清了场。除了南初这边，来参加婚礼的基本都是从小看着林陆骁长大的前辈，在他们这帮小辈里，林陆骁算是结婚结得早的。

this head is noisy, it is not easy over there, the wedding is relatively low-key, the media reporters are all blocked out of the door, lin qingyuan sent someone to clear the scene earlier. in addition to the nanchu side, the basic people who came to the wedding were the seniors who grew up watching lin luxiao, and among their juniors, lin luxiao was considered to have married early.

就比如大刘跟沈牧，两个单身铁汉。

for example, da liu and shen mu, two single iron men.

林陆晓这婚礼一打头，几个长辈也就顺手捞着大刘跟沈牧还柯孙明杨一块儿说道了：“这林陆骁都结婚了，你们几个也紧着点。”

lin luxiao this wedding nodded, a fewthe elder also said with a hand that liu and shen mu and kesun mingyang said, "this lin luxiao is married, and you guys are also tight."

被催得急了，大刘忍不住回嘴：“也得遇上个像嫂子这样漂亮的啊。”

being urged to be anxious, da liu couldn't help but reply: "i also have to meet a beautiful sister-in-law."

“你惦记我媳妇？”林陆骁冷不丁一眼，把大刘瞧慌神了，忙摇头，“哥，我哪敢？”

"do you miss my daughter-in-law?" lin luxiao glanced at him coldly, looked at da liu in a panic, and shook his head busily, "brother, how dare i?"

虽这么说着，白天几个小辈的接亲闹闹，几个长辈都没参加。全是大刘几个跟西顾带着玩了一天，南初安安静静地坐在房间里。

that being said, during the day, several juniors made a fuss about their relatives, and several elders did not participate. it was all a day of playing with xi gu, and nan chu sat quietly in the room.

林陆骁趁着哥儿个被西顾缠着打牌，直接溜进南初的房间。

lin luxiao took advantage of the fact that his brother was pestered by xi gu to play cards, and directly slipped into nan chu's room.

被眼尖的大刘雎瞧个正着，“骁爷也太沉不住气了。”

liu ju, who was sharp-eyed, looked at him squarely, "xiao ye is also too deep to breathe."

孙明杨道：“你家里要放着这么个漂亮的新娘，你能沉得住气？”

sun mingyang said, "you want to have such a beautiful bride in your home, can you hold your breath?"

大刘觉得有道理，点点头，倒也确实。

da liu felt that it made sense and nodded, but it was true.

南初今天确实美，就连刚进门的林陆骁都觉得有点惊艳，按理说，这张脸瞧了那么多遍，看了那么多遍，至少放在今天该有点免疫了。

nanchu is really beautiful today, even lin luxiao, who just entered the door, feels a little amazing, it is reasonable to say that this face has been looked at so many times, and has seen so many times, at least today it should be a little immune.

可刚才进门的瞬间，他脑子还是轰的一声，被击中了——真漂亮。

but the moment he entered the door just now, his brain still thundered, and he was hit - it was really beautiful.

这可是他媳妇几，舍不得给人瞧一眼。

this is his daughter-in-law, reluctant to give people a look.

不过林陆骁到底还是林陆骁，就算被惊艳到了，也始终只是嘴角噙着笑，抱着双臂靠在门边。

nolin luxiao was still lin luxiao in the end, even if he was amazed, he always just smiled at the corner of his mouth and leaned against the door with his arms.

南初就觉得这丫有点太不会来事了，她说：“你就不知道夸一句？”

nan chu felt that this girl was a little too unproductive, and she said, "you don't know how to boast?"

林陆骁抱臂倚着门，笑得欠扁，道：“这么明显的事还要我说？”

lin luxiao leaned against the door with his arm around him, smiled a little, and said, "do you want me to say such an obvious thing?"

“你说一下会死吗？”

"do you say you're going to die?"

林陆骁于是就低头笑，不说话。

lin luxiao then looked down and smiled and did not speak.

不光是林陆骁，就连南初也被门口的男人给帅到了。

not only lin luxiao, but even nanchu was handsome by the man at the door.

对于林陆骁来说，他的衣服儿乎是淸一色的军装、休闲服、黑色冲锋衣、羽绒服。南初见过他工作时的各种模样，也见过他私底下的模样。

for lin luxiao, his clothes are military uniforms, casual clothes, black storm jackets, and down jackets. nan chu had seen all kinds of things he looked like at work, and had also seen his appearance in private.

他比较偏好穿休闲，像这种正经的服装、别说西装，就连衬衫都没见他穿过几次。

he prefers to wear casual clothes, like this kind of serious clothing, not to mention suits, and even shirts have not been seen to wear a few times.

今天这个西装队长真是有点把她帅到了。

today this suit captain really made her a bit handsome.

果然，男人还是穿西装最带感，白衬衫十分贴合他的身材，就连胸肌都被勾勒出一点弧度，一条精致的皮带勒出了腰身，底下是一双修长的长腿，脚上是定制棕色尖头皮鞋。

sure enough, the man still wears the most feeling of the suit, the white shirt is very suitable for his figure, even the chest muscles are outlined a little curved, a delicate belt is stretched out of the waist, under the bottom is a pair of slender long legs, and the feet are custom brown pointed leather shoes.

再加上胸前的领带，禁欲感十足，每一分都勾勒得十分完美。

coupled with the tie on the chest, the ascetic feeling is complete, and every point is perfectly outlined.

这对南初来说，就姓赤|裸裸的诱惑。

for nanchu, the surname naked | naked temptation.

—直以来，她的认知就很清楚，这男人，确实很勾人。

— all along, her cognition has been very clear, this man, indeed very hooked.

（5）

仪式结束，酒席散，大刘、沈牧几个还嚷嚷着不肯散，林清远带着秘书先走了，临走时把林陆骁单独喊了出去。

after the ceremony was over, the banquet dispersed, da liu and shen mu were still clamoring and refusing to disperse, lin qingyuan took the secretary and left first, and when he left, he called lin luxiao out alone.

他一直也觉得从小这儿子跟自己就不亲，没承想转眼就结婚成了家，再过不久也许立马就要给他添个小孙子或孙女。这会儿再看林陆骁，那眼神倒一改往日的责备，而是在看一个真真正正的男人。

he has always felt that since he was a child, this son will not be close to him, and he will marry and become a family in the blink of an eye, and he may immediately add a little grandson or granddaughter to him soon. at this moment, looking at lin luxiao again, that look changed the previous rebuke, but was looking at a real and genuine man.

林清远说：“林启的工作怎么样了？”

lin qingyuan said: "what happened to lin qi's work?"

林陆骁今晚喝了不少，眼神有些微颤地说：“刘叔说给他找了个企业试试。”

lin luxiao drank a lot tonight, and his eyes trembled slightly: "uncle liu said to find him a company to try."

“真不拉琴了？”

"i really don't play the piano anymore?"

“这得问他，他真要喜欢，兴许干不久就回去拉琴了。”

"i have to ask him, he really likes it, maybe he will go back to playing the piano soon."

林清远了然地点点头，“也行，你照拂着点，这小子对什么事都不爱跟我说。”

lin qingyuan nodded his head, "okay, you take care of it, this boy doesn't like to tell me anything."

“嗯。”

"hmm."

说完林清远又不放心地叮嘱了几句：“今晚别太过了，闹闹差不多就得了，大刘几个没边，你得收着点，你可是有媳妇儿的人了。”

after saying that, lin qingyuan did not feel at ease and said a few words: "don't go too far tonight, the trouble is almost enough, the big liu has no edge, you have to collect some, you are a person with a daughter-in-law."

林陆骁难得苦笑，“这可由不得我。”

lin luxiao rarely smiled bitterly, "this is not up to me."

林清远拍拍他的肩膀走了。

lin qingyuan patted him on the shoulder and left.

林陆骁送完儿个长辈回到宴会厅的时候，才知道出事了。

when lin luxiao returned to the banquet hall after sending his children and elders, he knew that something had happened.

（6）

婚礼举行到九点，长辈们基本经不住几个小辈这么折腾，不到九点就走了，就剩下大刘这帮打小在巷子里一起长大的弟兄，还有一桌林陆骁队里的兄弟。

the wedding was held until nine o'clock, and the elders basically couldn't withstand the toss of a few juniors, and they left before nine o'clock, leaving the brothers who grew up together in the alley, and the brothers in lin luxiao's team.

这些可都不是好糊弄的主儿，一个个正敲着碗等他回去大干三百回合。

these are not fools, one by one, knocking on the bowl and waiting for him to go back to do three hundred rounds.

林陆骁被叫走，大家都把火力转向了南初，但大刘想着刚骁爷走前拍着他的膀子在他耳边低声让他照顾点他媳妇儿，别给人欺负了去。

lin luxiao was called away, and everyone turned their fire to nanchu, but da liu thought that grandpa gang xiao had just patted his arm and whispered in his ear to let him take care of his daughter-in-law and not to bully people.

大刘拼了命也是要护住南初的，谁灌都不让喝，非得说让等骁爷回来。

da liu desperately wanted to protect nan chu, and no one would let him drink, so he had to say that he would wait for xiao ye to come back.

就这么干晾了几分钟，大刘嘴碎，嘴上也没个把儿，一股脑儿就说起以前跟骁爷在巷子里犯浑的亊，还顺嘴说了当年在巷子口拉过一个小姑娘的事。

it was dried for a few minutes, the big liu mouth was broken, there was no handle on the mouth, a brain talked about the previous mess with xiao ye in the alley, and said smoothlyi pulled a little girl at the mouth of the alley that year.

大刘丝毫没意识到身旁的南初脸已经僵了，直到沈牧提他，他才恍然大悟。

da liu didn't realize that nan chu's face beside him had stiffened, until shen mu mentioned him, he suddenly realized.

“既然那女明星是南月如，那当时的小姑娘不就是一一南初？”

"since the female star is nan yueru, isn't the little girl at that time a nanchu?"

孽缘啊孽缘。

evil fate, evil fate.

可再收嘴已经来不及了，大刘干笑两声，刚要说话，就见林陆骁从外回来，他讪讪地往边上靠。

but it was too late to close his mouth again, da liu gan laughed twice, just about to speak, he saw lin luxiao returning from outside, he leaned to the side curtly.

林陆骁倒也没察觉出这尴尬的气氛，走过去，顺势就搂住南初的腰，“累吗。”

lin luxiao did not perceive this awkward atmosphere, walked over, and shunshi wrapped his arms around nan chu's waist, "tired."

南初扯扯嘴角，“不累。”

nanchu pulled the corners of his mouth, "not tired.

然后林陆骁难得低头在南初脸上亲了一下，当下就惊了好多人，就连赵国的媳妇儿都吓傻了眼，从不喜欢在公众场合秀恩爱表现亲密的男人忽然来这么一下，还真让人嫉妒，重点是这身西装帅得令人发指。而且，今晚这婚礼的阵仗也十分明显，这人并不她口中的穷屌丝，这身份还有得考究。

then lin luxiao rarely bowed his head and kissed nanchu's face, and at the moment he shocked many people, even zhao guo's daughter-in-law was frightened and dumbfounded, and he never liked to show his affection in public when a man who suddenly came to such a moment, and it was really jealous, the focus was that this suit was handsome and outrageous. moreover, the battle of this wedding tonight is also very obvious, this person is not the poor dick in her mouth, this identity is still exquisite.

方晴捅了捅赵国的胳膊，“我说你这兄弟到底什么来头？”

fang qing stabbed zhao guo's arm, "i said what the hell is going on with your brother?"

赵国哪知道，他也是前阵才听队长说的，“不太清楚，他姥爷……吧。”

zhao guona knew that he had only heard the captain say a while ago, "i don't know, his grandfather... right.

而那位姥爷也就在婚礼开始的时候露了个面儿，吃了两口就匆匆携老伴走了。

and the grandfather also showed his face at the beginning of the wedding, ate two bites and hurried away with his wife.

但据说，新婚闹洞房夜，英勇神武的骁爷，连门都没进去，在沙发上窝了一晚。

but it is said that the newlyweds made a cave room night, and the heroic and heroic xiao ye did not even enter the door and nestled on the sofa for one night.
